<script>
    $(document).ready(function(){
        var timeout;

		$('.block-suggester-container').on('click',function(e){

			e.stopPropagation();

        });

        $('.block-suggester-container .suggester input[type=text]').keyup(function(){
            var self = $(this);

            if(timeout) clearTimeout(timeout);

            timeout = setTimeout(function(){
                $.nette.ajax({
                    url: "https:\/\/www.kosik.cz\/poctive-piti?do=suggester-suggest",
                    data: {
                        phrase: self.val()
                    }
                })
            }, 300);


        });

    });

    function gaPush(self, cat)
    {
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'ga.pageview',
            'pagePath': '/hledat?q='+$('#frm-suggester-suggester-phrase').val()+'&cat='+cat,
            'pageTitle': 'Našeptávač'
        });

        window.location = self.href;
    }
</script>

</form>

    </div>

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('.region-navigation ul > li.sub').hover(function () {
                    var isOpen = $(this).data().open;

                    if (!isOpen) {
                        var images = $(this).find('img');

                        images.each(function (index, element) {
                            $(element).attr('src', $(element).data().src);
                        });

                        $(this).data().open = true;
                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

                var mobileMenu = $('#big-menu');

	<script async>
        $(document).ready(function () {
            var isOpen = $('body').hasClass('show');

            $('.region-recipes-makeYourself-carousel-inner .recipes-carousel').not('.slick-initialized').slick({
                dots: true,
                dotsClass: 'slick-dots slick-dots-hp',
                infinite: true,
                slidesToShow: 1,
                slidesToScroll:1,
                speed: 700,
            });

            $('.zone-microsite .basic-recomendation .recomendation-carousel-inner').slick({
                infinite: true,
                speed: 700,
                slidesToShow: isOpen ? 4 : 5,
                slidesToScroll: isOpen ? 4 : 5,
                responsive: [
                    {
                        breakpoint: 1025,
                        settings: {
                            slidesToShow: 4,
                            swipeToSlide: true
                        }
                    },
                    {
                        breakpoint: 769,
                        settings: {
                            slidesToShow: 3,
                            swipeToSlide: true
                        }
                    },
                    {
                        breakpoint: 560,
                        settings: {
                            slidesToShow: 2,
                            swipeToSlide: false,
                            slidesToScroll: 2,
                        }
                    },
                    {
                        breakpoint: 360,
                        settings: {
                            slidesToShow: 1,
                            slidesToScroll:1
                        }
                    }
                ]
            });

            fixing.onClose(function () {
                $('.zone-microsite .basic-recomendation .recomendation-carousel-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 5, true);
                $('.recipes-carousel').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 1, true);
            });

            fixing.onOpen(function () {
                $('.zone-microsite .basic-recomendation .recomendation-carousel-inner').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 4, true);
                $('.recipes-carousel').slick('slickSetOption', 'slidesToShow', 1, true);
            });

            $('.region-tabs-carousel .tab-carousel').click(function () {
                var block = $(this).data('tab');
                $('#'+block).siblings().removeClass('active');
                $('#'+block).addClass('active');
            });
        });

        function showFullContent(evt) {
            var parent = evt.currentTarget.parentNode.parentNode;
            parent.classList.toggle("show-full-content");
        }
	</script>
